***примирить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:примирить.html>примири́ть</a> (24936)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мирить.html>мири́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mirítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:примирить.html>примири́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">primirítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мирить.html>мири́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">примиря́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to reconcile</li>
<li>to conciliate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:примирить.html>примири́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:противоречивый.html>противоречи́вые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:точка.html>то́чки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зрение.html>зре́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>primirítʹ</b> protivorečívyje tóčki zrénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to reconcile contradictory views</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:примирить.html>примири́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:противоречивый.html>противоречи́вые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:требование.html>тре́бования</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>primirítʹ</b> protivorečívyje trébovanija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to balance the conflicting claims</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:примирить.html>примири́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">primirítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:примириться.html>примири́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">primirítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мириться.html>мири́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">примиря́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be reconciled <i>(with smb)</i>, to make up <i>(with smb)</i></li>
<li>to reconcile oneself
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:примириться.html>примири́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:положение.html>положе́нием</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>primirítʹsja</b> so svoím položénijem</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to reconcile oneself to the situation</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:примириться.html>примири́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:факт.html>фа́ктом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>primirítʹsja</b> s fáktom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">accept the fact</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:примирить.html>примири́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">primirítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:примкнувший.html>примкну́вший</a> (15442)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:примкнувший.html>примкну́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">primknúvšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:примкнуть.html>примкну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">primknútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-мкнуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-mknutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:примкнуть.html>примкну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">primknútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:примыкать.html>примыка́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to affix, to join together, to close

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to join ranks, to side with someone; to stand next to</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to include amongst</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-мыка́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-mykátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:примыкать.html>примыка́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">primykátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:примкнуть.html>примкну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to join, to side <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:примкнуть.html>примкну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:штык.html>штыки́</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>primknútʹ</b> štykí!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fix bayonets!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to adjoin, to border, to abut
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:примыкающий.html>примыка́ющие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:организация.html>организа́ции</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>primykájuščije</b> organizácii</i> ― <span class="e-translation">related organizations</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">grammar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to adjoin</li></ol>

***принести.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:принести.html>принести́</a> (641)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>нести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принести.html>принести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prinestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приносить.html>приноси́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bring (by foot), to fetch ((transitive) to transport toward somebody/somewhere)</li>
<li>to yield, to bear</li>
<li>to offer <i>(apologies, thanks, etc.)</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прино́с</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prinós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>нёс</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ти.html>ти́</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 7b/b⑨.     <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>Вариа́нт</a> прош. деепр. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:принести.html>принёсши</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:являться.html>явля́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:устаревший.html>устаре́вшим</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:приносить.html>приноси́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>при-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-нес-</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ти</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:принизить.html>прини́зивший</a> (31654)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принизить.html>прини́зивший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prinízivšij</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приникнуть.html>прини́кнуть</a> (15967)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:никнуть.html>ни́кнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">níknutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приникнуть.html>прини́кнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">priníknutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приникать.html>приника́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to press oneself <i>(against)</i>, to press oneself close <i>(to)</i>, to nestle <i>(against, to)</i>, to nestle close <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:приникнуть.html>прини́кнуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́хом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>priníknutʹ</b> úxom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put one's ear (to)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***принимать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:принимать.html>принима́ть</a> (652)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нима́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принимать.html>принима́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prinimátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принять.html>приня́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to take
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:принимать.html>принима́ю</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ванна.html>ва́нну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>prinimáju</b> vánnu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I’m taking a bath</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:принимать.html>принима́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:экзамен.html>экза́мен</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prinimátʹ</b> ekzámen</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to examine</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to admit, to accept
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Мы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:принять.html>при́мем</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:член.html>чле́нов</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">My <b>prímem</b> nóvyx člénov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">We’ll accept new members</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:принимать.html>принима́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:предложение.html>предложе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prinimátʹ</b> predložénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to accept an offer</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to receive
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:принимать.html>принима́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:гость.html>госте́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prinimátʹ</b> gostéj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">receive visitors</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:принимать.html>принима́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:радиоволна.html>радиово́лны</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prinimátʹ</b> radiovólny</i> ― <span class="e-translation">receive radiowaves</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to assume</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:мать.html>ма́ть</a></b>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-приним-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***приниматься.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приниматься.html>принима́ться</a> (3575)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принимать.html>принима́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prinimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приниматься.html>принима́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prinimátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приняться.html>приня́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to start doing something
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завтра.html>за́втра</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:приняться.html>приму́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́ги</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:университетский.html>университе́тской</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:программа.html>програ́мме</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Závtra <b>primúsʹ</b> čitátʹ knígi po universitétskoj prográmme.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Tomorrow I'll start reading books on the university program.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to take root
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посмотреть.html>посмо́трим</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:приняться.html>при́мутся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:саженец.html>са́женцы</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Posmótrim, <b>prímutsja</b> li sážency.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Let's see if the seedlings will take root.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принимать.html>принима́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prinimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:приняться.html>приня́ться</a>.
